<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>

<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>

<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>
<s> carey    january 5 1880 <\s>

<s> 93 bastiats    harmonies   conomiques    appeared in 1850 and the question of his indebtedness to carey was discussed rather unfavorably to bastiat in a series of letters in the    journal des   conomistes    for 1851 <\s>
<s> 94 see an able study by adolphe held    careys socialwissenschaft und das merkantilsystem    1866 <\s>
<s> 95 his system appears also in the books of disciples e <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>

<s> 94 see an able study by adolphe held    careys socialwissenschaft und das merkantilsystem    1866 <\s>
<s> 95 his system appears also in the books of disciples e <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>
<s> carey    january 5 1880 <\s>

<s> 94 see an able study by adolphe held    careys socialwissenschaft und das merkantilsystem    1866 <\s>
<s> 95 his system appears also in the books of disciples e <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>
<s> carey    january 5 1880 <\s>
<s> the latter gives a list of his books <\s>
<s> 93 bastiats    harmonies   conomiques    appeared in 1850 and the question of his indebtedness to carey was discussed rather unfavorably to bastiat in a series of letters in the    journal des   conomistes    for 1851 <\s>
<s> 94 see an able study by adolphe held    careys socialwissenschaft und das merkantilsystem    1866 <\s>
<s> 95 his system appears also in the books of disciples e <\s>
<s> peshine smith    a manual of political economy    1853 william elders    questions of the day    1871 and of robert e <\s>
<s> thompsons    social science and national economy    1875 <\s>
<s> a condensation of careys    social science    has been made by kate mckean in one volume octavo <\s>
<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>
<s> carey    january 5 1880 <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>

<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>
<s> see    proceedings of the american academy of science    1881 1882 p <\s>
<s> elders    memoir of henry c <\s>
<s> carey    january 5 1880 <\s>
<s> the latter gives a list of his books <\s>
<s> 93 bastiats    harmonies   conomiques    appeared in 1850 and the question of his indebtedness to carey was discussed rather unfavorably to bastiat in a series of letters in the    journal des   conomistes    for 1851 <\s>
<s> 94 see an able study by adolphe held    careys socialwissenschaft und das merkantilsystem    1866 <\s>
<s> 95 his system appears also in the books of disciples e <\s>
<s> peshine smith    a manual of political economy    1853 william elders    questions of the day    1871 and of robert e <\s>
<s> thompsons    social science and national economy    1875 <\s>
<s> a condensation of careys    social science    has been made by kate mckean in one volume octavo <\s>
<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>

<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>

<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>

<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>

<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>

<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>

<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>

<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>

<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>

<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>

<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>

<s> 92 carey 1793 1879 was the son of an irish exile and began a business career at the age of twelve <\s>
<s> at twenty eight he was the leading partner in the publishing firm of carey lea philadelphia from which he retired in 1835 to devote himself wholly to political economy <\s>
<s> his leading works have been translated into french italian portuguese german swedish russian magyar and japanese <\s>
<s> he has written thirteen octavo volumes three thousand pages in pamphlet form and twice that amount for the newspaper press <\s>

<s> 96 the son of amasa walker and formerly professor of political economy and history in the sheffield scientific school of yale college he has become well known for his statistical work in connection with the united states census <\s>
<s> his    statistical atlas of the united states    1874 is unequaled <\s>
<s> he has also published    money    1878 );    money trade and industry    1879 );    political economy    1883 ); and    land and rent    1884 <\s>
<s> the last book replies to various attacks on ricardos doctrine of rent and particularly to henry georges    progress and poverty    general walker in 1883 became president of the massachusetts institute of technology in boston <\s>
<s> he is also well known as an advocate of bimetallism <\s>
<s> 97 professor of political and social science in yale college and author of a    history of american currency    1874 );    lectures on the history of protection in the united states    1877 );    what social classes owe to each other    1883 <\s>
<s> he is a monometallist and has devoted himself vigorously to the advocacy of free trade <\s>
<s> his last book is a study in sociology not in political economy <\s>
<s> 98 he has written    political economy    eighteenth edition 1883 and also    introduction to political economy    an elementary work on the same basis as the former <\s>
<s> 99 henry george was born in philadelphia 1839 ran away to sea and in 1857 entered a printing office in san francisco <\s>
<s> in 1871 he was one of the founders of the    san francisco post    which he gave up in 1875 and received a public office <\s>
<s> he first began to agitate his views in a pamphlet entitled    our land and land policy    1871 but not until the comparative leisure of his occupation 1875 gave him opportunity did he seriously begin the study which resulted in his    progress and poverty    this volume was begun in the summer of 1877 and finished in the spring of 1879 <\s>
<s> the sale of the book it is needless to say has been phenomenal <\s>
<s> he has also applied his doctrine of land to ireland in a pamphlet entitled    the irish land question    1882 <\s>
<s> his last book is a collection of essays entitled    social problems    1884 <\s>
<s> his home is now in new york <\s>
